CREATE SEQUENCE user_id_seq
  INCREMENT 1
  MINVALUE 1
  MAXVALUE 9223372036854775807
  START 3
  CACHE 1;
  
 CREATE SEQUENCE advert_id_seq
  INCREMENT 1
  MINVALUE 1
  MAXVALUE 9223372036854775807
  START 1
  CACHE 1;
  
  CREATE SEQUENCE category_id_seq
  INCREMENT 1
  MINVALUE 1
  MAXVALUE 9223372036854775807
  START 6
  CACHE 1;
  
CREATE TABLE app_user
(
  id bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT nextval('user_id_seq'::regclass),
  sso_id character varying(30) NOT NULL,
  password character varying(100) NOT NULL,
  first_name character varying(30) NOT NULL,
  last_name character varying(30),
  email character varying(30) NOT NULL,
  role character varying(20),
  CONSTRAINT app_user_pkey PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT app_user_sso_id_key UNIQUE (sso_id)
);

CREATE TABLE persistent_logins
(
  username character varying(64) NOT NULL,
  series character varying(64) NOT NULL,
  token character varying(64) NOT NULL,
  last_used timestamp without time zone NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT persistent_logins_pkey PRIMARY KEY (series)
);


CREATE TABLE coordinates
(
  wojewodztwo character varying(40),
  miasto character varying(40),
  kod_pocztowy character varying(7) NOT NULL,
  sz_geo numeric,
  dl_geo numeric,
  CONSTRAINT coordinates_pkey PRIMARY KEY (kod_pocztowy)
);


CREATE TABLE category
(
  category_id bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT nextval('category_id_seq'::regclass),
  name character varying(64) NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT category_pkey PRIMARY KEY (category_id)
);

CREATE TABLE advert
(
  id bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT nextval('advert_id_seq'::regclass),
  title character varying(100) NOT NULL,
  description character varying(1000),
  website character varying(50),
  address character varying(100),
  email character varying(30),
  phone character varying(20),
  status character varying(10),
  date date,
  postal_code character varying(10),
  category_id bigint,
  user_id integer,
  CONSTRAINT advert_pkey PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT advert_category_id_fkey FOREIGN KEY (category_id)
      REFERENCES category (category_id) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION
);

CREATE TABLE app_user
(
  id bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT nextval('user_id_seq'::regclass),
  login character varying(30) NOT NULL,
  password character varying(100) NOT NULL,
  first_name character varying(30) NOT NULL,
  last_name character varying(30),
  email character varying(30) NOT NULL,
  role character varying(20),
  CONSTRAINT app_user_pkey PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT app_user_sso_id_key UNIQUE (login)
);
